🔧 HOW TO ENHANCE THIS ENGINE
Add entries: open Airtable → apify_crunchbase_calendar for your fund_thesis angle. Each entry: exact Crunchbase industry enum + city + employee band. Use ultra-specific enums (e.g. “Hotel”, “Legal Tech”, “Electronic Health Record (EHR)”) — broad enums like “Travel” or “Financial Technology” return thousands of irrelevant results. Rotate cities across EU hubs each day (Paris, London, Berlin, Amsterdam, Madrid, Stockholm, Zurich). Country is auto-filled from the city — never add a separate country field.
